        <h2 class="x-weight-semibold ow-heading-1 ow-headinghelper-1">Reimagine the way you work with Microsoft 365 and Microsoft Teams</h2> 
       </div> 
       <div class="ow-centered ow-card-area" data-grid="col-12"> 
        <div class="ow-card-ctn-outer"> 
         <div class="ow-card-ctn-inner x-clearfix ow-full-hide"> 
          <div class="ow-card" aria-hidden="false" data-uppercase-ctas="false"> 
           <div class="ow-img-ctn"> <picture class="x-clearfix"> 
             <img alt="Person sitting on the floor holding a piece of clothing while speaking with four other individuals on a video call in Microsoft Teams." title="Person sitting on the floor holding a piece of clothing while speaking with four other individuals on a video call in Microsoft Teams." src="https://img-prod-cms-rt-microsoft-com.akamaized.net/cms/api/am/imageFileData/RWF4PK?ver=0523&amp;q=90&amp;h=330&amp;w=435&amp;b=%23FFFFFFFF&amp;aim=true" srcset="https://img-prod-cms-rt-microsoft-com.akamaized.net/cms/api/am/imageFileData/RWF4PK?ver=0523&amp;q=90&amp;h=330&amp;w=435&amp;b=%23FFFFFFFF&amp;aim=true, https://img-prod-cms-rt-microsoft-com.akamaized.net/cms/api/am/imageFileData/RWF4PK?ver=0523&amp;q=90&amp;h=660&amp;w=870&amp;b=%23FFFFFFFF&amp;aim=true 2x"> 
            </picture> 
           </div> 
           <div class="ow-text-ctn"> 
            <h3 class="ow-heading-2 x-weight-semibold ow-headinghelper-2">Be productive anywhere</h3> 
            <div class="c-paragraph-3">
             <p>Get work done and stay connected whether youre working remotely or onsite.</p> 
             <ul class="c-list"> 
              <li>Chat, call, and host meetings</li> 
              <li>Share documents in the cloud</li> 
              <li>Collaborate using Office apps</li> 
              <li>Connect via email and calendar</li> 
             </ul> 
            </div>

    <div id="coreui-contentrichblock-4qvk7re" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;faq4ContentRichBlock 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-contentrichblock&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m1r10a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r10a2&quot;}" data-module-id="Office.PillarTemplate|faqregion4|coreui-region|coreui-contentrichblock-4qvk7re|coreui-contentrichblock"> 
     <div data-grid="col-12" class="c-rich-content-block context-ucx"> 
      <h2>Frequently asked questions</h2> 
     </div> 
    </div> 
    <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68" data-m="{&quot;cN&quot;:&quot;faq4Drawer 1&quot;,&quot;cT&quot;:&quot;Module_coreui-collapsibledrawer&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;m2r10a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;r10a2&quot;}" data-module-id="Office.PillarTemplate|faqregion4|coreui-region|coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68|coreui-collapsibledrawer"> 
     <section class="cui-drawer"> 
      <div class="cui-header "> 
       <div class="cui-drawer-toggle"> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Expand all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn1m2r10a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:1,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r10a2&quot;}" class="f-expand c-action-toggle" name="Expand all" data-toggled-label="Expand all" aria-label="Expand all">Expand all</button> <span>|</span> <button data-m="{&quot;pid&quot;:&quot;Collapse all&quot;,&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn2m2r10a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:2,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r10a2&quot;}" class="f-collapse c-action-toggle" name="Collapse all" data-toggled-label="Collapse all" aria-label="Collapse all" disabled>Collapse all</button> 
       </div> 
       <div style="clear: both;"></div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn3m2r10a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:3,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r10a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68-collapsible-drawer0">What is Microsoft 365?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68-collapsible-drawer0" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Microsoft 365 is the productivity cloud designed to help each of us achieve what matters, in our work and life, with best-in-class Office apps, intelligent cloud services, and advanced security.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn4m2r10a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:4,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r10a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68-collapsible-drawer1">How is Microsoft 365 with Microsoft Teams helping customers adjust to remote work?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68-collapsible-drawer1" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p><a aria-label="View the remote work trend report" href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2163919" class="c-hyperlink">View the remote work trend report</a> to discover how people around the world are adjusting to full-time remote work.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn5m2r10a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:5,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r10a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68-collapsible-drawer2">What happened to Office 365 plans?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68-collapsible-drawer2" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p>Office 365 business plans are now Microsoft 365 business plans. The new name more accurately reflects the range of features and benefits youll receive. You still have the same great value and price, along with best-in-class Office apps, intelligent cloud services, and advanced security.&nbsp;</p> 
        <ul class="c-list"> 
         <li>Office 365 Business Essentials is now Microsoft 365 Business Basic.</li> 
         <li>Office 365 Business Premium is now Microsoft 365 Business Standard.</li> 
         <li>Microsoft 365 Business is now Microsoft 365 Business Premium.</li> 
         <li>Office 365 Business is now Microsoft 365 Apps for business.</li> 
        </ul> 
        <p>There are no price or feature changes for small and medium business plans as a result of the updated name.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <div class="c-drawer"> <button data-m="{&quot;id&quot;:&quot;nn6m2r10a2&quot;,&quot;sN&quot;:6,&quot;aN&quot;:&quot;m2r10a2&quot;}" class="c-glyph" tabindex="0" aria-controls="coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68-collapsible-drawer3">Can I learn more about the value I get with Microsoft 365?</button> 
       <div id="coreui-collapsibledrawer-vychm68-collapsible-drawer3" class="c-drawer-panel"> 
        <p class="c-paragraph-3"> </p>
        <p><a aria-label="Download the full comparison table." href="https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=2164213" class="c-hyperlink">Download the full plan comparison table</a>.</p> 
        <p></p> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </section> 
    </div> 
   </div>
